     1	"""Water self-ionization closure (Phase 6α — proton-condition variable).
     2	
     3	Replaces the H⁺ Nernst--Planck residual with the proton-condition
     4	residual on ``E = c_H − c_OH``, with the fast-equilibrium closure
     5	``c_OH(y) = Kw_eff · exp(−u_H(y))`` (logc) or
     6	``c_OH = Kw_eff · exp(em·z_H·φ − μ_H)`` (muh).  The conservative flux
     7	in either backend reduces to
     8	
     9	    J_E = −(D_H · c_H + D_OH · c_OH) · ∇μ_H_full
    10	        + (D_H · c_H − D_OH · c_OH) · ∇μ_steric
    11	
    12	(after using ``z_OH = −1`` and ``∇μ_OH = −∇μ_H + ∇μ_steric``), where
    13	``∇μ_H_full = ∇u_H + em·z_H·∇φ + ∇μ_steric``.
    14	
    15	The H⁺ primary variable (``u_H`` or ``μ_H``) is unchanged — only the
    16	H⁺ residual EQUATION is replaced; the BVs on ``u_H``/``μ_H`` at the
    17	bulk Dirichlet stay the same.  The BV electrode reaction in acid-form
    18	ORR consumes only H⁺ (not OH⁻), so the existing
    19	``F_res -= stoi[h_idx] * R_j * v_list[h_idx] * ds`` term puts
    20	``J_E · n = J_H · n`` at the electrode automatically — no per-reaction
    21	rewiring needed.
    22	
    23	OH⁻ also enters:
    24	
    25	* Poisson source as ``(−1) · c_OH``.
    26	* Bikerman packing as ``a_OH · c_OH`` inside ``A_dyn``.
    27	
    28	Default-off via ``solver_options['bv_convergence']['enable_water_ionization']``;
    29	the feature is gated at form-build time so the disabled path is byte-
    30	equivalent to the pre-Phase-6α stack.
    31	
    32	See ``docs/PHASE_6A_OH_WATER_IONIZATION_PLAN.md`` for the full design.
    33	"""
    34	from __future__ import annotations
    35	
    36	from dataclasses import dataclass
    37	from typing import Any
    38	
    39	import firedrake as fd
    40	
    41	
    42	@dataclass(frozen=True)
    43	class WaterIonizationBundle:
    44	    """UFL pieces produced by :func:`build_water_ionization_terms`.
    45	
    46	    Attributes
    47	    ----------
    48	    h_idx
    49	        Species index of H⁺ (z = +1) in the dynamic species list.
    50	    kw_eff_func
    51	        R-space Function holding the current K_w_eff value.  Updated
    52	        in-place by ``set_reaction_kw_eff_model`` during continuation.
    53	    d_oh_const, a_oh_const
    54	        UFL Constants for the OH⁻ diffusivity and Bikerman size.
    55	    c_oh_expr
    56	        Symbolic ``Kw_eff · exp(−u_H_clamped)`` UFL expression at the
    57	        current time level.  Caller threads this into the Poisson
    58	        source and (when steric) the Bikerman packing.
    59	    c_oh_prev_expr
    60	        Same expression but built from ``u_H_clamped_old`` for the
    61	        backward-Euler time term.
    62	    e_var_expr
    63	        ``c_H − c_OH`` at the current time level (the proton-condition
    64	        variable).
    65	    e_var_prev_expr
    66	        ``c_H_old − c_OH_old`` at the previous time level.
    67	    """
    68	
    69	    h_idx: int
    70	    kw_eff_func: Any
    71	    d_oh_const: Any
    72	    a_oh_const: Any
    73	    c_oh_expr: Any
    74	    c_oh_prev_expr: Any
    75	    e_var_expr: Any
    76	    e_var_prev_expr: Any
    77	
    78	
    79	def resolve_h_index(z_vals, *, roles=None) -> int:
    80	    """Return the index of H⁺ in a dynamic species list.
    81	
    82	    Two paths:
    83	
    84	    * ``roles=None`` (legacy) — infer from ``z_vals``: exactly one
    85	      species with ``z = +1`` is required.  Raises with a descriptive
    86	      message otherwise so config errors fail loudly at form-build time
    87	      rather than silently mis-wiring c_OH.
    88	    * ``roles is not None`` (Phase 6β v9 Gate 1) — pick the unique index
    89	      whose role label is ``"proton"``.  Required when multiple
    90	      dynamic species share ``z = +1`` (the K2SO4 stack: H⁺ + K⁺).
    91	    """
    92	    if roles is not None:
    93	        if len(roles) != len(z_vals):
    94	            raise ValueError(
    95	                f"resolve_h_index: roles length {len(roles)} != z_vals "
    96	                f"length {len(z_vals)}; pass one role per dynamic species."
    97	            )
    98	        candidates = [
    99	            i for i, r in enumerate(roles)
   100	            if str(r).strip().lower() == "proton"
   101	        ]
   102	        if not candidates:
   103	            raise ValueError(
   104	                "resolve_h_index: no species with role='proton' in "
   105	                f"roles={list(roles)}."
   106	            )
   107	        if len(candidates) > 1:
   108	            raise ValueError(
   109	                "resolve_h_index: multiple species with role='proton' in "
   110	                f"roles={list(roles)} (indices {candidates}); roles must "
   111	                "be unique."
   112	            )
   113	        return candidates[0]
   114	
   115	    candidates = [i for i, zv in enumerate(z_vals) if abs(float(zv) - 1.0) < 1e-12]
   116	    if not candidates:
   117	        raise ValueError(
   118	            "enable_water_ionization=True requires a species with z=+1 (H+); "
   119	            f"none found in z_vals={list(z_vals)}."
   120	        )
   121	    if len(candidates) > 1:
   122	        raise ValueError(
   123	            "enable_water_ionization=True requires exactly one species with "
   124	            f"z=+1 (H+); found {len(candidates)} (indices {candidates})."
   125	        )
   126	    return candidates[0]
   127	
   128	
   129	def build_water_ionization_terms(
   130	    *,
   131	    ctx: dict,
   132	    conv_cfg: dict,
   133	    z_vals,
   134	    u_h_unclamped,
   135	    u_h_unclamped_prev,
   136	    ci_h_clamped,
   137	    ci_h_prev_clamped,
   138	    R_space,
   139	    u_clamp: float,
   140	    roles=None,
   141	) -> WaterIonizationBundle:
   142	    """Build the OH⁻ closure expressions used by the proton-condition residual.
   143	
   144	    The H⁺ log-concentration expression (``u_h_unclamped``) is the
   145	    pre-clamp value; the same symmetric clamp ``[-u_clamp, u_clamp]``
   146	    applied to ``c_H = exp(u_h_unclamped)`` is applied to ``-u_H`` to
   147	    bound ``c_OH = Kw_eff · exp(-u_H)``.  Because the clamp is symmetric
   148	    about zero, ``clamp(-x) = -clamp(x)``, so passing the already-built
   149	    ``ci_h_clamped`` (which uses the same symmetric clamp) and dividing
   150	    is byte-equivalent — but the explicit ``exp(-u_clamped)`` form keeps
   151	    the algebra parallel to the existing ``ci`` pattern and avoids
   152	    a divide-by-near-zero at quadrature points where ``ci_h_clamped``
   153	    underflows to ``exp(-100)`` ≈ 3.7e-44.
   154	
   155	    Parameters
   156	    ----------
   157	    ctx
   158	        Firedrake context.  Mutated in place: ``ctx['water_ionization']``
   159	        is set to the returned bundle for downstream Q3 / diagnostics.
   160	    conv_cfg
   161	        ``solver_options['bv_convergence']`` sub-dict.  Reads
   162	        ``enable_water_ionization`` (must be True; caller gates),
   163	        ``kw_eff_hat``, ``d_oh_hat``, ``a_oh_hat``.
   164	    z_vals
   165	        Per-species charge list.  Used to locate the H⁺ index.
   166	    u_h_unclamped, u_h_unclamped_prev
   167	        UFL expressions for ``ln(c_H)`` at the current and previous
   168	        time levels.  In ``forms_logc.py`` these are ``ui[h_idx]`` and
   169	        ``ui_prev[h_idx]``; in ``forms_logc_muh.py`` they are the
   170	        reconstructed ``μ_H − em·z_H·φ`` expressions.
   171	    ci_h_clamped, ci_h_prev_clamped
   172	        UFL expressions for ``c_H = exp(clamp(u_H))`` at the two time
   173	        levels.  Caller has already built these for the dynamic-species
   174	        residual; we reuse them in ``E = c_H − c_OH`` to keep the time
   175	        derivative consistent with the rest of the species.
   176	    R_space
   177	        ``firedrake.FunctionSpace(mesh, "R", 0)`` for the Kw_eff
   178	        Function.
   179	    u_clamp
   180	        Symmetric clamp magnitude (typically 100.0 in production).
   181	
   182	    Returns
   183	    -------
   184	    WaterIonizationBundle
   185	    """
   186	    h_idx = resolve_h_index(list(z_vals), roles=roles)
   187	
   188	    kw_eff_initial = float(conv_cfg.get("kw_eff_hat", 0.0))
   189	    d_oh = float(conv_cfg.get("d_oh_hat", 0.0))
   190	    a_oh = float(conv_cfg.get("a_oh_hat", 0.0))
   191	
   192	    if d_oh <= 0.0:
   193	        raise ValueError(
   194	            f"enable_water_ionization=True but d_oh_hat={d_oh!r} is non-positive; "
   195	            "set bv_convergence['d_oh_hat'] to the OH⁻ nondim diffusivity."
   196	        )
   197	    if kw_eff_initial < 0.0:
   198	        raise ValueError(
   199	            f"enable_water_ionization=True but kw_eff_hat={kw_eff_initial!r} "
   200	            "is negative; the continuation ladder may start at 0 but cannot "
   201	            "go below."
   202	        )
   203	
   204	    kw_eff_func = fd.Function(R_space, name="kw_eff_water_ionization")
   205	    kw_eff_func.assign(kw_eff_initial)
   206	
   207	    d_oh_const = fd.Constant(d_oh)
   208	    a_oh_const = fd.Constant(a_oh)
   209	
   210	    u_clamp_c = fd.Constant(float(u_clamp))
   211	    neg_u_clamp_c = fd.Constant(-float(u_clamp))
   212	
   213	    # c_OH = Kw_eff · exp(-u_H), with the same symmetric clamp on -u_H
   214	    # as on u_H.  Because the clamp is symmetric, clamp(-u_H) = -clamp(u_H)
   215	    # and we could equivalently write Kw_eff / ci_h_clamped — but the
   216	    # explicit exp form preserves the existing ``ci`` algebra structure.
   217	    neg_u_h_clamped = fd.min_value(
   218	        fd.max_value(-u_h_unclamped, neg_u_clamp_c), u_clamp_c
   219	    )
   220	    neg_u_h_prev_clamped = fd.min_value(
   221	        fd.max_value(-u_h_unclamped_prev, neg_u_clamp_c), u_clamp_c
   222	    )
   223	
   224	    c_oh_expr = kw_eff_func * fd.exp(neg_u_h_clamped)
   225	    c_oh_prev_expr = kw_eff_func * fd.exp(neg_u_h_prev_clamped)
   226	
   227	    e_var_expr = ci_h_clamped - c_oh_expr
   228	    e_var_prev_expr = ci_h_prev_clamped - c_oh_prev_expr
   229	
   230	    bundle = WaterIonizationBundle(
   231	        h_idx=int(h_idx),
   232	        kw_eff_func=kw_eff_func,
   233	        d_oh_const=d_oh_const,
   234	        a_oh_const=a_oh_const,
   235	        c_oh_expr=c_oh_expr,
   236	        c_oh_prev_expr=c_oh_prev_expr,
   237	        e_var_expr=e_var_expr,
   238	        e_var_prev_expr=e_var_prev_expr,
   239	    )
   240	    ctx["water_ionization"] = bundle
   241	    return bundle
   242	
   243	
   244	def build_proton_condition_flux(
   245	    *,
   246	    bundle: WaterIonizationBundle,
   247	    D_h,
   248	    c_h,
   249	    ideal_grad_h,
   250	    mu_steric_grad,
   251	    steric_active: bool,
   252	):
   253	    """Return ``J_E = J_H − J_OH`` for the proton-condition residual.
   254	
   255	    Uses the identities (z_H = +1, z_OH = −1, em·z_H = +1):
   256	
   257	    * ``∇ln(c_OH) + em·z_OH·∇φ = −∇u_H − em·∇φ = −(∇u_H + em·∇φ)``
   258	      — so the OH⁻ "ideal gradient" is exactly the negation of the
   259	      H⁺ ideal gradient.
   260	    * Steric chemical potential ``μ_steric = −ln(θ)`` is the same
   261	      activity correction for every dynamic species, so OH⁻ picks up
   262	      the SAME ``+∇μ_steric`` term as H⁺.
   263	
   264	    The conservative NP flux is therefore
   265	
   266	        J_E = −(D_H·c_H + D_OH·c_OH)·∇μ_ideal
   267	              − (D_H·c_H − D_OH·c_OH)·∇μ_steric
   268	
   269	    (both flux contributions linear in ``∇μ_ideal`` and ``∇μ_steric``
   270	    separately; the steric correction cancels except where the
   271	    diffusivity-weighted balance ``D_H·c_H ≠ D_OH·c_OH`` is broken).
   272	
   273	    **Sign convention.**  Both forms files build the dynamic-species
   274	    residual block as
   275	
   276	        F_res += ((c_i − c_old)/dt) · v · dx + dot(Jflux, ∇v) · dx
   277	
   278	    which assembles the weak form ``∫(∂c/∂t)·v − ∫J_NP·∇v + ∫J_NP·n·v``
   279	    (integration by parts of ``∇·J_NP``) ONLY when the symbol ``Jflux``
   280	    holds the *negation* of the true Nernst-Planck flux, i.e.
   281	    ``Jflux = −J_NP = +D·c·∇μ``.  See ``forms_logc.py`` line 334 (or
   282	    ``forms_logc_muh.py`` line 440): ``D · c · ∇μ`` is written with a
   283	    POSITIVE sign — that is the convention this helper must match.
   284	    Returning ``-J_E`` here keeps the same convention so callers can
   285	    write ``F_res += dot(<this expression>, ∇v) dx`` unchanged.
   286	
   287	    Parameters
   288	    ----------
   289	    bundle
   290	        Output of :func:`build_water_ionization_terms`.  Provides the
   291	        OH⁻ diffusivity Constant and the c_OH expression.
   292	    D_h
   293	        H⁺ diffusivity expression (typically ``fd.exp(logD_funcs[h_idx])``).
   294	    c_h
   295	        H⁺ concentration expression (``ci[h_idx]``).
   296	    ideal_grad_h
   297	        ``∇μ_H_ideal`` for the H⁺ species — i.e. ``∇u_H + em·z_H·∇φ``
   298	        in logc, ``∇μ_H`` in muh.
   299	    mu_steric_grad
   300	        ``∇μ_steric`` UFL expression, or ``None`` when ``steric_active``
   301	        is False.
   302	    steric_active
   303	        Caller-provided flag; matches the existing ``steric_active``
   304	        gate in both forms files.
   305	
   306	    Returns
   307	    -------
   308	    UFL expression for ``-J_E`` (= the residual-side ``Jflux`` symbol
   309	    for the proton-condition variable).  At ``Kw_eff = 0`` (so c_OH = 0)
   310	    this reduces algebraically to the H⁺ NP residual the form would
   311	    have built without water-ionization, restoring byte-equivalence at
   312	    the continuation floor.
   313	    """
   314	    d_oh = bundle.d_oh_const
   315	    c_oh = bundle.c_oh_expr
   316	
   317	    flux = (D_h * c_h + d_oh * c_oh) * ideal_grad_h
   318	    if steric_active and mu_steric_grad is not None:
   319	        flux = flux + (D_h * c_h - d_oh * c_oh) * mu_steric_grad
   320	    return flux
   321	
   322	
   323	def is_water_ionization_enabled(conv_cfg: dict) -> bool:
   324	    """Centralized gate check; reads the ``enable_water_ionization`` flag.
   325	
   326	    Returns False both when the key is missing (legacy params dict) and
   327	    when set to a falsy value, so callers can rely on a uniform default.
   328	    """
   329	    return bool(conv_cfg.get("enable_water_ionization", False))
   330	
   331	
   332	__all__ = [
   333	    "WaterIonizationBundle",
   334	    "build_proton_condition_flux",
   335	    "build_water_ionization_terms",
   336	    "is_water_ionization_enabled",
   337	    "resolve_h_index",
   338	]

   322	    #
   323	    # The clamp is applied to the reconstructed log(c_H), not raw mu_H,
   324	    # so the floating-point overflow protection on c_H = exp(...) is
   325	    # preserved for the muh formulation.
   326	    _U_CLAMP = float(conv_cfg.get("u_clamp", 30.0))

   333	        return ui_split[i]

   363	            u_h_unclamped_prev=u_prev_exprs[h_idx_water],
   364	            ci_h_clamped=ci[h_idx_water],
   365	            ci_h_prev_clamped=ci_prev[h_idx_water],
   366	            R_space=R_space,
   367	            u_clamp=_U_CLAMP,
   368	            roles=species_roles,
   369	        )
   370	    else:
   371	        h_idx_water = None
   372	        water_bundle = None
   373	
   374	    # Electrode potential constant.
   375	    phi_applied_func = fd.Function(R_space, name="phi_applied")
   376	    phi_applied_func.assign(float(scaling["phi_applied_model"]))
   377	    phi0_func = fd.Function(R_space, name="phi0")
   378	    phi0_func.assign(float(scaling["phi0_model"]))
   379	
   380	    # Global E_eq.
   381	    E_eq_model_global = fd.Constant(float(scaling["bv_E_eq_model"]))
   382	    bv_exp_scale = fd.Constant(float(scaling["bv_exponent_scale"]))
   383	
   384	    # Stern layer flag.
   385	    stern_capacitance_model = scaling.get("bv_stern_capacitance_model")
   386	    use_stern = stern_capacitance_model is not None and float(stern_capacitance_model) > 0
   387	
   388	    def _build_eta_clipped(E_eq_const):
   389	        """Build clipped overpotential expression for a given E_eq.
   390	
   391	        See ``forms_logc.py`` for the full semantics of the clip.
   392	        """
   393	        if use_stern:
   394	            eta_raw = phi_applied_func - phi - E_eq_const
   395	        elif conv_cfg["use_eta_in_bv"]:
   396	            eta_raw = phi_applied_func - E_eq_const
   397	        else:
   398	            eta_raw = phi - E_eq_const
   399	        eta_scaled = bv_exp_scale * eta_raw
   400	        if conv_cfg["clip_exponent"]:
   401	            clip_val = fd.Constant(float(conv_cfg["exponent_clip"]))
   402	            return fd.min_value(fd.max_value(eta_scaled, -clip_val), clip_val)
   403	        return eta_scaled
   404	
   405	    eta_clipped = _build_eta_clipped(E_eq_model_global)
   406	
   407	    # Steric chemical potential (Bikerman model) -- ci[mu_h_idx] is the
   408	    # muh-reconstructed c_H, so packing automatically uses the right c_H.
   409	    a_vals_list = [float(v) for v in a_vals]
   410	    steric_a_funcs = [fd.Function(R_space, name=f"steric_a_{i}") for i in range(n)]
   411	    for i in range(n):
   412	        steric_a_funcs[i].assign(float(a_vals_list[i]))
   413	
   414	    # Steric-aware analytic Boltzmann counterion(s) — same Option 2
   415	    # wiring as forms_logc.py: closure expression must enter BOTH
   416	    # Poisson AND the dynamic species' total packing fraction.
   417	    c0_model_for_steric = scaling.get("c0_model_vals", c0_raw)
   418	    steric_boltz = build_steric_boltzmann_expressions(
   419	        ctx=ctx,
   420	        params=params,
   421	        ci=ci,
   422	        a_dyn_funcs=steric_a_funcs,
   423	        a_dyn_floats=a_vals_list,
   424	        c0_dyn=[float(v) for v in c0_model_for_steric[:n]],
   425	        z_dyn=[int(v) for v in z_vals[:n]],
   426	        phi=phi,
   427	        R_space=R_space,
   428	    )
   429	
   430	    steric_active = (
   431	        any(v != 0.0 for v in a_vals_list)
   432	        or bool(steric_boltz)
   433	        or (water_ion_enabled and float(water_bundle.a_oh_const) != 0.0)
   434	    )
   435	    if steric_active:
   436	        packing_floor = float(conv_cfg.get("packing_floor", 1e-8))
   437	        A_dyn = sum(steric_a_funcs[j] * ci[j] for j in range(n))
   438	        if water_ion_enabled and float(water_bundle.a_oh_const) != 0.0:
   439	            # OH⁻ Bikerman packing contribution (shadow species).
   440	            A_dyn = A_dyn + water_bundle.a_oh_const * water_bundle.c_oh_expr
   441	        if steric_boltz:
   442	            # Multi-counterion: shared z_scale, sum packing_contribution
   443	            # over every bikerman bundle.  Single-counterion case (the
   444	            # legacy path) reduces to the same UFL algebra.
   445	            z_scale_shared = steric_boltz[0].z_scale
   446	            packing_total = sum(b.packing_contribution for b in steric_boltz)
   447	            theta_inner = (
   448	                fd.Constant(1.0) - A_dyn - z_scale_shared * packing_total
   449	            )
   450	        else:
   451	            theta_inner = fd.Constant(1.0) - A_dyn
   452	        packing = fd.max_value(theta_inner, fd.Constant(packing_floor))
   453	        mu_steric = -fd.ln(packing)
   454	
   455	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   456	    # Residual: Nernst-Planck with muh transform
   457	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   458	    # For non-mu species (u_i = log(c_i)):
   459	    #   J_i = -D_i * c_i * (grad(u_i) + em*z_i*grad(phi))
   460	    # For mu species (mu_H = u_H + em*z_H*phi):
   461	    #   J_H = -D_H * c_H * grad(mu_H)
   462	    # because grad(u_H) + em*z_H*grad(phi) = grad(mu_H) by definition.
   463	    F_res = 0
   464	
   465	    for i in range(n):
   466	        c_i = ci[i]
   467	        c_old = ci_prev[i]
   468	        v = v_list[i]
   469	
   470	        if i in mu_species:
   471	            # mu-species flux: D*c*grad(mu) (+ steric activity).  In muh,
   472	            # the proton's μ_H is the primary, so ∇μ_H_ideal = ∇ui[i].
   473	            ideal_grad = fd.grad(ui[i])
   474	        else:
   475	            # log-c flux: D*c*(grad(u) + em*z*grad(phi))
   476	            drift = fd.Constant(em) * z[i] * phi
   477	            ideal_grad = fd.grad(u_exprs[i]) + fd.grad(drift)
   478	
   479	        if water_ion_enabled and i == h_idx_water:
   480	            # Phase 6α — proton-condition residual on E = c_H − c_OH for
   481	            # the muh backend.  ``ideal_grad`` here is ∇μ_H (the primary).
   482	            mu_steric_grad = fd.grad(mu_steric) if steric_active else None
   483	            Jflux = build_proton_condition_flux(
   484	                bundle=water_bundle,
   485	                D_h=D[i],
   486	                c_h=c_i,
   487	                ideal_grad_h=ideal_grad,
   488	                mu_steric_grad=mu_steric_grad,
   489	                steric_active=steric_active,
   490	            )
   491	            F_res += (
   492	                (water_bundle.e_var_expr - water_bundle.e_var_prev_expr)
   493	                / dt_const
   494	            ) * v * dx
   495	            F_res += fd.dot(Jflux, fd.grad(v)) * dx
   496	            continue
   497	
   498	        if steric_active:
   499	            Jflux = D[i] * c_i * (ideal_grad + fd.grad(mu_steric))
   500	        else:
   501	            Jflux = D[i] * c_i * ideal_grad
   502	
   503	        # Time-stepping residual: (c - c_old)/dt
   504	        F_res += ((c_i - c_old) / dt_const) * v * dx
   505	        F_res += fd.dot(Jflux, fd.grad(v)) * dx
   506	
   507	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   508	    # Butler-Volmer boundary flux
   509	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   510	    # Surface concentrations are c_surf[i] = ci[i] -- already muh-aware
   640	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   641	    suppress_poisson_source = _bool(nondim_cfg.get("suppress_poisson_source", False))
   642	    eps_coeff = fd.Constant(float(scaling["poisson_coefficient"]))
   643	    charge_rhs = fd.Constant(float(scaling["charge_rhs_prefactor"]))
   644	    F_res += eps_coeff * fd.dot(fd.grad(phi), fd.grad(w)) * dx
   645	    if not suppress_poisson_source:
   646	        F_res -= charge_rhs * sum(z[i] * ci[i] * w for i in range(n)) * dx
   647	        if water_ion_enabled:
   648	            # OH⁻ Poisson contribution (z = −1).
   649	            F_res -= charge_rhs * (
   650	                fd.Constant(-1.0) * water_bundle.c_oh_expr
   651	            ) * w * dx
   652	        if steric_boltz:
   653	            # Bikerman counterion charge density: shared z_scale, sum
   654	            # charge_density across every bundle.  Single-counterion
   655	            # case reduces to the same UFL algebra as the legacy path.
   656	            z_scale_shared = steric_boltz[0].z_scale
   657	            charge_density_total = sum(b.charge_density for b in steric_boltz)
   658	            F_res -= (
   659	                z_scale_shared * charge_rhs * charge_density_total * w * dx
   660	            )
   661	
   662	    # Stern layer Robin BC.  Phase 6β v9 Gate 2: ``stern_coeff`` is
   663	    # promoted to the ctx so the C_S continuation ladder in
   664	    # ``solve_anchor_with_continuation`` can reassign it via
   665	    # ``set_stern_capacitance_model``.
   666	    if use_stern:
   667	        stern_coeff = fd.Constant(float(stern_capacitance_model))
   668	        F_res -= stern_coeff * (phi_applied_func - phi) * w * ds(electrode_marker)
   669	    else:
   670	        stern_coeff = None
   671	
   672	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   673	    # Phase 6β v9 Gate 3 — cation hydrolysis (Γ as external coefficient)
   674	    # ---------------------------------------------------------------
   675	    cation_hydrolysis_bundle = None

     1	"""Formulation dispatcher for the BV-PNP forward solver.
     2	
     3	The production stack uses the log-concentration backend (``forms_logc``).
     4	An experimental proton-electrochemical-potential variant
     5	(``forms_logc_muh``) is available for ``formulation="logc_muh"``; the muh
     6	backend stores the proton primary variable as ``mu_H = u_H + em*z_H*phi``
     7	to give Newton a smoother variable in Debye-layer regions where ``u_H``
     8	and ``phi`` separately vary by tens of log-units.  See
     9	``Forward/bv_solver/forms_logc_muh.py`` for the math and
    10	``docs/electrochemical_potential_solver_plan.md`` for the landing plan.
    11	
    12	``build_context`` / ``build_forms`` / ``set_initial_conditions`` dispatch on:
    13	
    14	  - ``params['bv_convergence']['formulation']``  -- selects backend module
    15	    (``"logc"`` or ``"logc_muh"``).
    16	  - ``params['bv_convergence']['initializer']``  -- selects IC routine
    17	    within the chosen backend (``"linear_phi"`` or ``"debye_boltzmann"``).
    18	
    19	The ``*_logc`` and ``*_logc_muh`` names are re-exported for scripts that
    20	want to be explicit about the backend they target.
    21	"""
    22	
    23	from __future__ import annotations
    24	
    25	from typing import Any
    26	
    27	from .forms_logc import (
    28	    build_context_logc,
    29	    build_forms_logc,
    30	    set_initial_conditions_logc,
    31	    set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc,
    32	)
    33	from .forms_logc_muh import (
    34	    build_context_logc_muh,
    35	    build_forms_logc_muh,
    36	    set_initial_conditions_logc_muh,
    37	    set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc_muh,
    38	)
    39	
    40	
    41	def _read_bv_convergence_field(solver_params: Any, key: str, default: str) -> str:
    42	    """Read ``bv_convergence[key]`` with a graceful default.
    43	
    44	    Robust to ``SolverParams`` (via ``__getitem__``), legacy 11-tuples,
    45	    and malformed test inputs.  Falls back to ``default`` whenever the
    46	    config block is missing or non-dict.
    47	    """
    48	    try:
    49	        params_dict = solver_params[10] if hasattr(solver_params, "__getitem__") else None
    50	    except Exception:
    51	        params_dict = None
    52	    if not isinstance(params_dict, dict):
    53	        return default
    54	    bv_conv = params_dict.get("bv_convergence", {})
    55	    if not isinstance(bv_conv, dict):
    56	        return default
    57	    return str(bv_conv.get(key, default)).strip().lower()
    58	
    59	
    60	def _read_formulation(solver_params: Any) -> str:
    61	    return _read_bv_convergence_field(solver_params, "formulation", "logc")
    62	
    63	
    64	def _read_initializer(solver_params: Any) -> str:
    65	    return _read_bv_convergence_field(solver_params, "initializer", "linear_phi")
    66	
    67	
    68	def _resolve_backend(solver_params: Any) -> str:
    69	    """Pick a backend module name based on ``formulation``.
    70	
    71	    Returns one of ``"logc"`` or ``"logc_muh"``.  Unknown formulations
    72	    fall through to ``"logc"`` (the production default) -- the config
    73	    layer (``Forward/bv_solver/config.py:_validate_formulation``) already
    74	    rejects unknown names at parse time, so this is defensive only.
    75	    """
    76	    formulation = _read_formulation(solver_params)
    77	    if formulation == "logc_muh":
    78	        return "logc_muh"
    79	    return "logc"
    80	
    81	
    82	def build_context(solver_params: Any, *, mesh: Any = None) -> dict:
    83	    backend = _resolve_backend(solver_params)
    84	    if backend == "logc_muh":
    85	        return build_context_logc_muh(solver_params, mesh=mesh)
    86	    return build_context_logc(solver_params, mesh=mesh)
    87	
    88	
    89	def build_forms(ctx: dict, solver_params: Any) -> dict:
    90	    backend = _resolve_backend(solver_params)
    91	    if backend == "logc_muh":
    92	        return build_forms_logc_muh(ctx, solver_params)
    93	    return build_forms_logc(ctx, solver_params)
    94	
    95	
    96	def set_initial_conditions(
    97	    ctx: dict, solver_params: Any, *, blob: bool = False
    98	) -> None:
    99	    """Set initial conditions for the dispatched backend.
   100	
   101	    Dispatches on ``params['bv_convergence']['formulation']`` to pick the
   102	    backend, then on ``params['bv_convergence']['initializer']`` to pick
   103	    the IC routine within that backend:
   104	
   105	      - ``"linear_phi"``     -> ``set_initial_conditions_*``
   106	      - ``"debye_boltzmann"`` -> ``set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_*``
   107	
   108	    ``blob`` is accepted for backward-compatible kwargs and silently
   109	    ignored -- blob ICs were a concentration-formulation feature removed
   110	    with that backend.
   111	    """
   112	    backend = _resolve_backend(solver_params)
   113	    initializer = _read_initializer(solver_params)
   114	    if backend == "logc_muh":
   115	        if initializer == "debye_boltzmann":
   116	            return set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc_muh(ctx, solver_params)
   117	        return set_initial_conditions_logc_muh(ctx, solver_params)
   118	    if initializer == "debye_boltzmann":
   119	        return set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc(ctx, solver_params)
   120	    return set_initial_conditions_logc(ctx, solver_params)
   121	
   122	
   123	__all__ = [
   124	    "build_context",
   125	    "build_forms",
   126	    "set_initial_conditions",
   127	    # logc backend (production)
   128	    "build_context_logc",
   129	    "build_forms_logc",
   130	    "set_initial_conditions_logc",
   131	    "set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc",
   132	    # logc_muh backend (experimental)
   133	    "build_context_logc_muh",
   134	    "build_forms_logc_muh",
   135	    "set_initial_conditions_logc_muh",
   136	    "set_initial_conditions_debye_boltzmann_logc_muh",
   137	]

189:del _math_aspec, _AVOGADRO_ASPEC, _A_O2_PHYS, _A_H2O2_PHYS, _A_HP_PHYS
216:# Diffusivity (Atkins / CRC 25 °C):  D_OH⁻ = 5.273e-9 m²/s.
220:D_OH = 5.273e-9              # m²/s
222:# C_SCALE / D_REF / L_REF are defined above; KW_HAT / D_OH_HAT / A_OH_HAT
225:D_OH_HAT = D_OH / D_REF
246:    d_ref: float = D_REF,
401:# H2O2 is initialised at a small positive seed (1e-4) to keep ln(c0)
403:H2O2_SEED_NONDIM = 1e-4
407:    d_vals_hat=[D_O2_HAT, D_H2O2_HAT, D_HP_HAT],
410:    a_vals_hat=[A_O2_HAT, A_H2O2_HAT, A_HP_HAT],
411:    c0_vals_hat=[C_O2_HAT, H2O2_SEED_NONDIM, C_HP_HAT],
425:# ``boltzmann_counterions=None`` in ``make_bv_solver_params``.  H+ and
432:    d_vals_hat=[D_O2_HAT, D_H2O2_HAT, D_HP_HAT, D_CLO4_HAT],
437:    a_vals_hat=[A_O2_HAT, A_H2O2_HAT, A_HP_HAT, A_DEFAULT],
438:    c0_vals_hat=[C_O2_HAT, H2O2_SEED_NONDIM, C_HP_HAT, C_CLO4_HAT],
491:        (e.g. ``0.16`` ≈ 16 µm at L_REF = 100 µm) to test the H+ Levich
512:        ``D_OH_HAT`` / ``A_OH_HAT`` (5.273e-9 m²/s and r=1.76 Å Marcus).
548:        "diffusivity_scale_m2_s": D_REF,

661:        # species set has at least 3 species (i.e. tracks H+ explicitly), unless

797:D_KPLUS_HAT = D_KPLUS / D_REF

872:# H+ stoichiometric concentration factor is included on each reaction

1212:        L_eff transport sweep vary the H+ Levich ceiling without

codex
1. WHAT: `TestWaterRouteEscapesLevichCap` asks for `|cd| > 10x` the 15.4 µm H+ cap. That is about `>5.8 mA/cm2`, above or equal to the 4e O2 Levich ceiling `~5.7`.
WHY: The test is physically impossible or will only pass through a bug.
WHAT to do: Use a threshold like `>3-5x H+ cap` and also assert `<= O2 4e ceiling`.

2. WHAT: The plan says species Levich-film differences are `<=10%`. False for ions. With repo constants, `D_H+/D_O2 ~4.9`, so `delta_H/delta_O2 ~1.7`; `OH-` is `~1.4`.
WHY: H+/OH transport, local pH, and caps are materially wrong under a single O2 film.
WHAT to do: Add a species-specific Levich sensitivity or stop calling this a 10% error.

3. WHAT: Sulfate/bisulfate buffering is absent. At pH 4 in sulfate electrolyte, inert `SO4^2-` is not enough chemistry.
WHY: A water route generates OH- at one OH per electron. Without buffer, pH will likely run too alkaline, and cation hydrolysis may get blamed for missing bulk buffer physics.
WHAT to do: Add/estimate `HSO4-/SO4^2-` buffer capacity before fitting, or prove it is negligible by flux scale.

4. WHAT: “Water routes share E_eq by thermodynamics” is overstated. The proposed water route has no OH/product factors and is irreversible.
WHY: That is not a thermodynamically consistent alkaline BV law; it is an empirical cathodic Tafel branch.
WHAT to do: Either derive the alkaline BV form in model variables, or explicitly call `E_eq` a formal onset parameter and do not use thermodynamic language.

5. WHAT: “Zero weak-form edits” misses the observable layer. Existing `gross_h2o2_current` returns one reaction index, not `R2e_acid + R2e_water`.
WHY: The fit will silently use the wrong peroxide current unless every driver avoids the helper.
WHAT to do: Add a summed-reaction observable or `h2o2_reaction_indices`, with tests.

6. WHAT: Per-reaction “currents” are ambiguous. `mode="reaction", scale=-I_SCALE` gives a 2e-scaled rate; it is wrong for 4e current.
WHY: Reported R4e current will be off by 2x and per-reaction sums will not match total disk current.
WHAT to do: Output both molar rates and electron-weighted currents: `-I_SCALE * (n_e/2) * R_j`.

7. WHAT: Validation likely still uses an old diffusion limit. `assemble_observable_validated` fails any observable above `I_lim`.
WHY: Water-route success is defined by exceeding the H+ cap, so valid runs can be flagged invalid/dropped.
WHAT to do: Make `I_lim` route/observable aware: O2 4e for total, O2 2e for H2O2, not H+ cap.

8. WHAT: Acid `R2e` remains reversible, but the plan says no surface consumption of free H2O2.
WHY: The net `R_j = cathodic - anodic` can consume H2O2 and distort the anodic flank.
WHAT to do: Either make deck-topology R2e irreversible or expose cathodic-only and anodic-only rates and define the RRDE observable explicitly.

9. WHAT: The proposed mechanism says pH drives 2e-to-4e branching, but water 2e and water 4e are both pH-independent.
WHY: The volcano may come from O2 competition/Tafel slopes, not local pH. That breaks the paper mechanism.
WHAT to do: Add pH-clamped, O2-unlimited, water2e-only, and water4e-only ablations before claiming attribution.

10. WHAT: Hydrolysis continuation is under-specified. Existing infrastructure rejects `lambda_hydrolysis_ladder` combined with `kw_eff_ladder`/`c_s_ladder`.
WHY: Stage 2 cannot just “add k_hyd/lambda” inside the current continuation flow.
WHAT to do: Specify and test the sequence: Kw ramp at `lambda=0`, Stern bump, then separate lambda ramp.

11. WHAT: R3 says `E_eq 1.76 V OCP-shifted`, while the convention says all E_eq values are shifted centrally.
WHY: This invites a double shift for the 5th reaction.
WHAT to do: Store all E_eq values unshifted vs RHE and apply the OCP shift in one place, with an eta-preservation test.

12. WHAT: The fit is underdetermined: 4 water parameters fit one H2O2 curve, while total current and local pH are only “validation.”
WHY: You can fit the volcano with wrong current partition and wrong pH.
WHAT to do: Include disk current and pH-vs-current as hard constraints or objective terms, and report parameter identifiability.

13. WHAT: The coarse sweep varies only k0 factors, then may reject the mechanism if shape is wrong.
WHY: Peak position can be alpha-sensitive; a k0-only reconnaissance can falsely reject a viable branch.
WHAT to do: Add a small alpha grid or sensitivity pass before the “shape wrong” gate.

14. WHAT: Digitization sigma from line thickness is not experimental uncertainty, and dense downsampled curve points are correlated.
WHY: WLS will overweight artwork smoothness and plateau length.
WHAT to do: Fit independent marker/trace bins, separate digitization error from experimental error, or use block/correlated weights.

15. WHAT: Water-route validation in `dispatch.py::build_forms` is too late and too narrow.
WHY: Scripts/tests can build forms through multiple backends, and parser/nondim can already propagate bad configs.
WHAT to do: Centralize reaction validation after parsing, cover both `logc` and `logc_muh`, and test water-route + water-ionization-off failures.

16. WHAT: The plan has no global OH/E balance diagnostic.
WHY: With `E = c_H - c_OH`, acid H+ consumption and water OH- production are algebraically indistinguishable; pH alone cannot prove the route is physically behaving.
WHAT to do: Add integrated boundary source, E-flux, OH production/removal, and acid/water current-share checks at every voltage.

VERDICT: ISSUES_REMAIN
